 var postal_code;var reserve_id;var reserve_label;var params=getSearchParameters();if(params.from_reserve=='mobile'&&params.postal_code!=''){if(params.reserve_id!=''&&params.reserve_label!=''){$("#selectedReserve").val(decodeURI(params.reserve_label));$("#reservedid").val(params.reserve_id);setTimeout(function(){reserveDelivery(params.postal_code);},1000);}else{setTimeout(function(){$("#btn-check-reserve-mobile").click();},1000);}}function checkDelivery(postalCode,status){if(typeof postalCode==="undefined"||postalCode==-1){postalCode=$('#check-delivery-postal-mobile').val();}if(postalCode.length!==6){bootbox.alert('Enter a valid 6-digit postal code');}else{dark_cover();var post_url='https://coldstorage.com.sg/checkout/cart/checkdelivery';postal_code=postalCode;$.post(post_url,{postal_code:postalCode},function(data){dark_uncover();obj=data;var strHtml='';strHtml=strHtml+'<p>Earliest available slot for <strong>'+postalCode+'</strong> is<br /><span class="date">'+fulldate+'</span>, <span Date(arrDayHeader[i]);if(earliestDay==weekday[date.getDay()]){strHtml=strHtml+"<div class='grid-15 selected'><span class='day-title'>"+weekday[date.getDay()]+'</span><br/>'+date.getDate()+' '+monthNames[date.getMonth()]+"</div>";}else{strHtml=strHtml+"<div class='grid-15'><span class='day-title'>"+weekday[date.getDay()]+'</span><br/>'+date.getDate()+' '+monthNames[date.getMonth()]+"</div>";}}strHtml=strHtml+"</div>"+'<div class="clearfix"> </div>';strHtml=strHtml+"<div class='timeslot-content'>";$.each(obj.timeslot,function(day,record){var dateSlot=new Date(day);strHtml=strHtml+"<div class='grid-15'>";keysSorted=Object.keys(record).sort();$.each(keysSorted,function(idx,time){strTimelabel=record[time].label;strTimeslotidx='"'+record[time].timeslot_idx+'"';strTimelabel=strTimelabel.replace(/:00/g,':00');strTimelabel=strTimelabel.replace(/.00/g,':00');strSelectTime='"'+weekday[dateSlot.getDay()]+" "+dateSlot.getDate()+' '+monthNames[date.getMonth()]+", "+strTimelabel+'"';if(record[time].available==true&&status=="yes"){if(params.reserve_id!=undefined&&params.reserve_id.toString()==record[time].timeslot_idx){strHtml=strHtml+"<a class='highlight enable' id='reserved_time' onclick='reserved("+strTimeslotidx+",this,"+strSelectTime+")' >"+strTimelabel+"</a><br/>";}else{strHtml=strHtml+"<a class='highlight enable' onclick='reserved("+strTimeslotidx+",this,"+strSelectTime+")' >"+strTimelabel+"</a><br/>";}}else if(record[time].available==true&&status=="no"){strHtml=strHtml+"<a class='highlight enable' href='javascript:void(0);'>"+strTimelabel+"</a><br/>";}else{strHtml=strHtml+"<a class='highlight disable'>"+strTimelabel+"</a><br/>";}});strHtml=strHtml+"</div>";});strHtml=strHtml+'</div>'+'<div $(".btn-register-mobile").click();});}},'json');}}function reserveDelivery(postalCode){var post_url=site_config.base_path+'checkout/cart/reserveTimeslot';$.post(post_url,{timeslot:$("#reservedid").val(),postal:postalCode},function(data){obj=JSON.parse(data);if(obj.valid){var notif='You have selected the following delivery slot: <b style="color: #00b050;">'+$("#selectedReserve").val()+'</b>';show_notif(notif);$('.text-reserve').html('Your delivery slot: <b>'+$("#selectedReserve").val()+'</b>').addClass('reserved');localStorage.setItem("reservedslot",$("#selectedReserve").val());$("#selectedReserve").val('');$("#reservedid").val('');reserve_slot.init();if(typeof normal_delivery_slot=='object'&&typeof checkout_cart=='object'){normal_delivery_slot.get_delivery_timeslot(checkout_cart.getActiveAddressPostalCode());}var newUrl=window.location.href.split('?')[0]
window.history.pushState("object or string","Title",newUrl);}else{if(typeof obj.message==="undefined"){show_notif('Failed to reserve.');}else{show_notif(obj.message);}$("#reservedid").val('');}});}function replaceUrlParam(url,paramName,paramValue){if(paramValue==null)paramValue='';url=url.replace('?name=','');var pattern=new RegExp('\\b('+paramName+'=).*?(&|$)')
if(url.search(pattern)>=0){return url.replace(pattern,'$1'+paramValue+'$2');}return url+(url.indexOf('?')>0?'&':'?')+paramName+'='+paramValue}function getSearchParameters(){var prmstr=window.location.search.substr(1);return prmstr!=null&&prmstr!=""?transformToAssocArray(prmstr):{};}function transformToAssocArray(prmstr){var params={};var prmarr=prmstr.split("&");for(var i=0;i<prmarr.length;i++){var tmparr=prmarr[i].split("=");params[tmparr[0]]=tmparr[1];}return params;}function reserved(timeslotIdx,elm,strSelectTime){reserve_id=timeslotIdx;reserve_label=strSelectTime;$("#reservedid").val(timeslotIdx);$("#selectedReserve").val(strSelectTime);$(".reserve-delivery-dialog-mobile .reserved").removeClass("reserved");$(elm).addClass("reserved");}$(function(){if(typeof localStorage.reservedslot!=="undefined"){$('.text-reserve').html('Your delivery slot: <b>'+localStorage.reservedslot+'</b>').addClass('reserved');}$(document).on('click','.timeslot-nav.left',function(){var val=$('.timeslot-wrapper').scrollLeft();val=parseInt(val)-142;$('.timeslot-wrapper').scrollLeft(val);});$(document).on('click','.timeslot-nav.right',function(){var val=$('.timeslot-wrapper').scrollLeft();val=parseInt(val)+142;$('.timeslot-wrapper').scrollLeft(val);});});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

addToShoppingList(element,type,cart_id){bootbox.hideAll();if(cart_id==undefined){var selIndex=$("#shopping-list-select-id option:selected").val();}else{var selIndex=cart_id;}if(selIndex>=0){dark_cover();var qty=0;if(type=='simple'){var qty=shopping_list_quantity;}else if(type=='configurable'){var qty=shopping_list_quantity;}if(qty>0){var
